Changelog

Date Author Change
2021-08-20 Bj√∂rn Esser <besser82 at fedoraproject dot org> - 1.12.0-1 - Disable fat-lto-objects to reduce memory usage Doing so will not hurt as we are not shipping any static libraries - Re-enable and realign oom patch - Update oom patch to fix multiple definition errors
